Ebu eme ahiḡe kurauꞌohe; Badiꞌa gigiꞌa inaraḡa ḡonaga ꞌoꞌoꞌa hina zaeꞌa inarifine, ebu eꞌe inaraḡa hina zaeꞌa mene ḡarihe maḡunifine, zu aduganiꞌa onaiteꞌea, zaeꞌa edau gigarafine, ebu zae zamao matuꞌuꞌa iriꞌavoga.
Ebu eme hena ahiḡe kurauꞌohe; Zaeꞌa Badiꞌa, emeḡe Mama mazao manoḡa tauḡi rouga. Badiꞌa ani, ane mone raꞌeteꞌe azaḡaniꞌa Badiꞌa haba agaḡa zamaḡano radiuꞌenaꞌa meꞌuma manohugaḡa, zae zuni zeḡe teite meifine, ibitoziniro.
Aꞌe Badiꞌaꞌa uzaboonoꞌo emeḡe mae vaḡifiro, ebu ane ubuga zamaroneḡaniꞌa zuhiꞌaniꞌeteꞌe zamaḡano ohofiro.
Ebu Badiꞌa ani Keriso ru hina emeḡe ḡabofiro, ebu emeḡe sauꞌa niduꞌa rae modiro.
Eme Badiꞌaꞌe horonoga mene idaḡa, rehano Iesu Kerisoꞌe Badiꞌa iraḡa fureneꞌohe. Iesu Kerisoꞌe, ḡau niduꞌa ize izema fureranogano Badiꞌa teite radiunu, ebu ḡau niduꞌaꞌe ani ꞌuꞌuḡano.
Mazaḡa Kerisonoꞌo Badiꞌa ḡau niduꞌa haḡairo, adure zu rahao radiuꞌeteꞌe ḡauḡa, horoneꞌeteꞌe zu horonoga mene idaḡa ḡauḡa haḡairo. Badiꞌaꞌa vine zuhiꞌaḡa, tuḡure viga inaraḡa ebu ḡau inaraḡa niduꞌa Kerisonoꞌo zu Keriso veize haḡairo.
Kerisoꞌe ḡau niduꞌa ize izema fureranogano aniꞌe ꞌeꞌe radiunu, ebu aniꞌa ḡau niduꞌa radiu onameꞌeteꞌe zu ḡau niduꞌa gaue tiburuꞌeteꞌe haḡairo.
Keriso ani ekalesia vadiga, ebu ekalesiaꞌe ani ahiri. Ḡadaheḡanoꞌe ḡau niduꞌa ani mazaonoꞌo fureraro, ebu aniꞌe runeonoꞌo ḡabodiꞌuma azaḡa boꞌaḡano aneꞌa ibite ḡabodiro. Aꞌe ḡau niduꞌa aneꞌa zuhiꞌanoga veize.
Mazaḡa Badiꞌa aniꞌe ane urao Keriso zamaḡano radiꞌuma reiro. Ebu eꞌanoꞌo Kerisoꞌa Badiꞌa haḡai furenehuniꞌuma.
Ebu Badiꞌaꞌa ane urao vaze zu ḡau niduꞌa Keriso teite bare tibuniꞌuma reiro. Ebu Badiꞌa zu ḡau niduꞌa boꞌaḡano zama roḡeḡa veize Kerisoꞌa satauroo ruḡa soniroteꞌeanoꞌo, adure zu rahao radiuꞌeteꞌe ḡauḡa niduꞌa, ibiteꞌe Badiꞌa mazao fararo rehano, Keriso teite bare tibuziro.
Zaꞌe ibitebone Badiꞌa mazaonoꞌo fararo, ebu zaꞌe haḡai sauꞌa haḡaidoteꞌe uꞌano, za zamaꞌe agireḡa radu, Badiꞌa mazaonoꞌo fararo.
Rehano Kerisoꞌa ane ahirio satauroo rudaroteꞌe uꞌano, izidi zaꞌe Badiꞌaꞌa ane teite bare tibuziro, zaꞌe ane zamao ohozadu, ane ubumao zaꞌe duduḡa, ebu toragani oꞌoꞌa reifine. Vazeꞌa Badiꞌa zamao zaꞌe veꞌoreha rae mene reꞌuma.
Zaeꞌa hubehune Badiꞌa mazao fie onameꞌenaꞌa edau gigaraune, zu hari manoḡa zamaḡano, ḡabone manoḡa meꞌuma reiroteꞌe ḡoeꞌa zaeꞌa obone giganine, zaꞌe Badiꞌa ubumao duduḡa reꞌuma. Eꞌe hariḡa manoḡaꞌe haba niduꞌa zamaḡano harame onaeha. Ebu eḡe, Pauloꞌe Badiꞌaꞌa hari manoḡa harameꞌeteꞌe gauḡano ohohiro.
Izidi ꞌada eꞌe, zae mazao hari manoḡa haramiroteꞌe uꞌano aduga hideꞌeteꞌe moneo matuꞌeꞌohe. Ebu Kerisoꞌa aduga hidiroteꞌe teiḡe, eḡe zuni eḡe ahiri hina eꞌe aduḡaḡa hideꞌeteꞌe mene rihoneꞌohe. Eꞌe haḡaiḡaꞌe Keriso ahiriꞌe ekalesia azaḡa veize.
Eꞌe Badiꞌaꞌa ekalesia azaḡa tuḡure gauḡano ohohiro. Aꞌe zae mazao, Badiꞌa ane ḡoere ihozoga veize
Uꞌuru radiuꞌeteꞌe ḡauḡa ꞌaꞌaꞌe amahi hune azaḡa mazao Badiꞌaꞌa mene rae fureniro, rehano izidi ane mone raꞌeteꞌe azaḡa mazao fureneꞌohe.
Badiꞌa ani, ibite mene rae fureniroteꞌe uꞌuru radiroteꞌe ḡauḡa manoḡa ꞌaꞌaꞌe, Iuda mene azaḡa boꞌaḡano Badiꞌa inahe meiroteꞌe azaḡa mazao rae fureniꞌuma reiro. Eꞌe uꞌuru radiroꞌeteꞌe ḡauḡaꞌe Keriso. Aniꞌe zae zamao radiuꞌohe, eꞌanoꞌo Badiꞌaꞌe manoḡa hune uꞌano zae zuni manoḡa hune reꞌuma.
Ebu emeꞌe edeḡafe niduꞌa hina iraduguzenaꞌa, zu ihozeꞌenaꞌa, vaze niduꞌa mazao Keriso hariḡa harameꞌohe, mazaḡa emeḡe uraꞌe emeḡeꞌa danazadu vaze niduꞌaꞌa Badiꞌa zama faifairu edereꞌenaꞌa, ane ibio daꞌo onameꞌenaꞌa duduḡa vazeḡa radu, Keriso ane zamao ohoziꞌuma.
ꞌOuge haḡaeꞌeteꞌe veize eḡe zamao inare gauꞌetaꞌe Keriso gigiꞌaḡa hina inare gauꞌeꞌohe.
Eḡeꞌa ꞌadi raꞌetaꞌaꞌe, e ura za ederoꞌi! Eḡeꞌa zae, zu Laodikea neḡa azaḡa, ebu ize mene horohateꞌe azaḡa niduꞌa danazoga veize inareꞌohe.
E ura zeꞌa inaratitoga zu zamarotiteꞌenaꞌa tiburanoga. Ebu e ura zeꞌa Badiꞌa uꞌuru ḡauḡa edere hunoga. Uꞌuru ḡauḡa aꞌe Keriso.
Ebu Keriso mazao buꞌu Badiꞌaꞌa uꞌuru tidoteꞌe zamaroneḡa boro bagaḡa ederiꞌuma.
Eḡeꞌa ꞌadi raꞌetaꞌaꞌe, vazeꞌa zamaguhi ḡoeꞌa hina mene soꞌozifine.
Ḡianoꞌi! Eꞌe zae teite mene radiuꞌe rehano, eḡe zamaꞌe zae mazao radiuꞌohe. Eꞌanoꞌo zaeꞌa haḡai manoḡano radiuꞌeteꞌe zu zaeꞌa Keriso mazao fie gigaruꞌeteꞌe ederadu, matuꞌeꞌohe.
Eꞌanoꞌo Keriso Iesuꞌe Zuhiꞌa Boro radu zaꞌe mae ḡihiniro ꞌahine, ani teite tiburu radiuꞌenoꞌi!
Ebu ire taiganiꞌa rahao kame gigaruꞌeteꞌe teige, Keriso mazao kame gigaranadu, ane zamareꞌenaꞌa farau onamoꞌi! Ebu Epafaraꞌa Badiꞌa ḡoere ihozidoteꞌe teige obone giganoꞌi! Ebu Badiꞌa mazao iḡaiḡa manoḡa tauḡi roꞌi!
Vaze ḡoere faine ḡianoꞌi! Hena, zeḡeꞌa tutuze veꞌoziꞌuma. Zeꞌe Badiꞌa edeḡa zu vazeꞌa nouge nouge radiuꞌeteꞌe edeḡa niduꞌa raha adi ibiḡano ihoziꞌuma. Zeḡe ḡoereꞌe huga ꞌoꞌoꞌa zu ḡuriro ḡoeꞌa. Ḡoere aꞌe Kerisoonoꞌo mene onaeꞌohe, rehano amahi azaḡa edeḡanonoꞌo zu haba ꞌadi vineḡanonoꞌo.
Ḡianoꞌi! Mazaḡa Badiꞌa ḡabone zu haḡai niduꞌaꞌe Keriso zamaḡano iriꞌave radiuꞌohe. Kerisoꞌe vaze reirotene aniꞌe ize Badiꞌa, eꞌanoꞌo zaꞌe Keriso zamaḡano Badiꞌa haḡai niduꞌa horoneꞌohe.
Ebu zaꞌe Keriso teite tibuziro zu ani mazaonoꞌo haḡai ꞌadi niduꞌa meiro. Vine sauꞌa zuhiꞌaḡa, zuhiꞌa niduꞌa zu ḡau niduꞌaꞌe Keriso ꞌuꞌuḡano radiuꞌohe.
Iuda azaḡaꞌe, Badiꞌa mone raꞌetene, vaze ꞌevore hina ahiri ogaḡa variꞌe modadu iḡuri haḡaeꞌohe. Eꞌe teige zaꞌe, Keriso mone reirotene, Kerisoꞌa zamaroneze sauꞌa zu ḡaboneze sauꞌa variꞌe modeꞌenaꞌa, zamazeo iḡuri haḡairo.
Eꞌe hugaꞌe, zaeꞌa Badiꞌa ni mae ḡihinadu bapatizo meiroteꞌe zamaḡano, Keriso teite ḡuriro, ebu Keriso ane teite bare ḡabode iḡuniro. Mazaḡa Badiꞌaꞌa Keriso runeonoꞌo bare ḡaboniroteꞌe gigiꞌaḡa mazao zaeꞌa firo ꞌahine.
Ebu ibite vinezeꞌe rudanoga zu Badiꞌa mazaonoꞌo faraunu. U eꞌe madaḡanoꞌe, zae ḡabone sauꞌaꞌe ize mene variꞌe modiro. Rehano ꞌouge ize haḡairoteꞌea, Badiꞌaꞌa zaꞌe Keriso teite bare ḡaboziro. Ebu emeḡe sauꞌa niduꞌa rae modiro.
Ebu Badiꞌaꞌe Emeḡe haḡai sauꞌa uꞌano emeḡe ꞌuteꞌeteꞌe Iuda azaḡa goro ḡoeꞌaꞌe niduꞌa madu, Keriso teite satauroniro. ꞌOuge haḡaeꞌenaꞌa, Badiꞌaꞌe goro ḡoeꞌa niduꞌa ꞌuiro.
Ebu ꞌouge haḡaeꞌenaꞌa, Badiꞌaꞌa vine sauꞌa zuhiꞌaḡa zu zuhuꞌa inaraze mae buno ziniro. Mazaḡa goro ḡoeꞌa ꞌuiro ꞌahine, Sataniꞌa eꞌe ḡoeꞌa hina emeḡe ꞌutoga mene idaḡa. Ebu Keriso satauroniroteꞌe zamaḡano, vine niduꞌa Kerisoꞌa roꞌaze hauḡiroteꞌe, Badiꞌaꞌa hunio fureniro.
Eanoꞌo, zaeꞌa aueꞌeteꞌe zu gageꞌeteꞌe moneo ga muri muiḡa, bato iziḡa muiḡa zu Iuda azaḡa Bana Madaḡa uꞌano, vaze ꞌahoganiꞌa zae veꞌoḡa rae zoitene gararozenoꞌi!
Mene! Iuda azaḡa goro ḡoeꞌa zu muiḡa ꞌuḡuḡaꞌe Badiꞌaꞌa rae tiroteꞌe ḡauḡa manoḡa emege rifiuma vineḡa isoḡa. Rehano izidi ḡau manoḡa aꞌe fureraneha. Eꞌe ḡauḡa hugaꞌe Keriso.
Ḡurireꞌenaꞌa nize mae ovoeꞌeteꞌe zu tuḡure viga mazao kurauꞌeteꞌe azaḡa ḡoere ago egoꞌi! Zeꞌe za tutuze veꞌozihi raꞌohe. Zeꞌe tuḡure viga horoneha raꞌenaꞌa, nize mae iteꞌenaꞌa ḡoeriꞌuma, rehano ze zamaꞌe mene Badiꞌa mazaonoꞌo, ebu ze ꞌane zeꞌe nize boro azaḡa reꞌuma.
Zeꞌe Keriso mene hegoteꞌohe. Keriso ani ekalesia vadiga, ekalesia azaḡaꞌe ane ahiꞌa. Aꞌuꞌa zu viniga hina tibuzetene ahiri niduꞌa gigazeꞌohe. Ebu Badiꞌaꞌa ekalesia ibitoziniꞌenaꞌa inariꞌuma.
Zaꞌe Keriso teite rudauꞌetene, raha ꞌadi vineḡa zuhiꞌaḡaonoꞌo mae buzeꞌohe. Rehano zaꞌe nougadu ize raha azaḡa haḡaio radiuꞌeteꞌe teige zeḡe ḡoere igiꞌohe?
Ze ꞌahige raꞌohe, “Ago obone toꞌi! Ago au nuroꞌi! Ago obone nuroꞌi!”
ꞌAhiguḡa goro ḡoeꞌaꞌe vaze mazaonoꞌo onaeꞌohe. Eꞌe goro ḡoeꞌaꞌe mene faḡa haḡaeꞌohe zu dauḡeꞌohe.
Goro ḡoeꞌa ꞌuguḡaꞌe edeḡa boro ḡoeꞌa iraḡa, rehano hugaꞌe oꞌoꞌa. Zeꞌa kuru veize zeḡe bare inahiroteꞌe ḡauḡaꞌe vaze mazaꞌonoꞌo zu zeꞌe ḡurireꞌenaꞌa nize ufeta mae ovoiꞌuma, ga ahirize sausauneꞌetaꞌe Badiꞌa matuo hafine. Rehano goro ḡoeꞌa ꞌuguḡaꞌe gigiꞌaḡa oꞌoꞌa ꞌahine, zamarone sauꞌa mae vaḡiniꞌuma moneo mene danazeꞌohe.
Goro ḡoeꞌa ꞌuguḡaꞌe gigiꞌaḡa oꞌoꞌa. Eꞌanoꞌo ḡabone ḡauḡa adureo radiuꞌeteꞌe daꞌo zamare borofeꞌenaꞌa vaḡoꞌi! Mazaḡa zaꞌe Keriso teite ḡabozadu, ḡabone iziga meiro. Ebu Keriso ani adureo Badiꞌa edaꞌe moneo inaraḡeta radiuꞌohe.
Eꞌanoꞌo adure ḡauḡa daꞌo zamaroꞌi! U raha ꞌadi ḡauḡaꞌe ago zamaroꞌi!
Mazaḡa zaꞌe ibiꞌa haḡaiḡa sauꞌa modiro, ebu zaꞌe Badiꞌa ꞌevore zamaḡano Keriso teite tiburu radiuꞌohe. Badiꞌa aḡuꞌa azaḡaꞌe eꞌe ederoga mene idaḡa.
Kerisoꞌe ḡabone iziga ziniꞌeteꞌe vazeḡa. Keriso aneꞌa bare onaiꞌuma madaḡano, zae zuni ani teite agaḡa manoḡano edaꞌuma.
Eꞌanoꞌo zaꞌe ahiriꞌa urateꞌeteꞌe haḡaiḡa niduꞌa mae mode hauḡoꞌi! Aꞌe ubuma ḡezo, zamarone toraga, ahiri uꞌuteꞌeteꞌe zamare borofeꞌeteꞌe, ḡau mae buroga urateꞌeteꞌe. Ebu ḡau ḡehaḡa ago urate rudanoꞌi, mazaḡa ꞌuguḡa vazeḡaꞌe ire emoga mazao kurauꞌeteꞌe heuḡa.
Eꞌe guḡa haḡaiḡa uꞌano Badiꞌaꞌe zamaḡa ḡugine runadu, eꞌe naeḡa ziniꞌuma.
Zae zuni ibite ꞌuguḡa haḡaiḡa haḡaeꞌeteꞌe azaḡa teite tiburu radiudo, ebu ꞌuguḡa haḡaiḡa haḡaido.
Rehano izidi zaꞌe, maḡunu, zama ḡugi, vaze sausauneꞌeteꞌe, vaze ni sausaune ḡoereꞌeteꞌe, ꞌuguḡa haḡaiḡa niduꞌa modoꞌi! Ebu ufire ḡoea zae hebeonoꞌo ago roꞌi!
Ebu vaze teite ago ḡurirotitoꞌi, mazaḡa zaꞌe sauꞌa haḡaoga urateꞌeteꞌe zamaroneḡa zu ibite raha ꞌada haḡairoteꞌe haḡaiḡa modiro,
ebu vaze iziga reiro. Badiꞌa ani, aneꞌa vaze haḡairoteꞌe iraḡa idunaḡano, zae izifeꞌohe, zaeꞌa Badiꞌa faifairu ederifine.
Badiꞌaꞌa ḡabone iziga rifiroteꞌe moneo, emeꞌe ꞌahige mene reꞌuma: Giriki azaḡa ga Iuda azaḡa, ahiꞌrio iḡuri haḡairoteꞌe azaḡa ga iḡuri mene haḡairoteꞌe azaḡa, guniꞌa azaḡa ga Sikute azaḡa, ḡuꞌa teige gauꞌeteꞌe azaḡa ga bohaꞌa azaḡa. ꞌOuge emeꞌe emeḡeꞌa bare avoavo mene rae reꞌuma. Rehano emeḡe niduꞌa Keriso mone raꞌeteꞌe daꞌo zamare borofiꞌuma. Kerisoꞌe emeḡe niduꞌa zamao radiuꞌohe.
Eꞌanoꞌo Badiꞌaꞌa ane mone raꞌeteꞌe azaḡa zu aneꞌa zamare borofeꞌeteꞌe azaḡa, zaꞌe, Badiꞌaꞌa ane veize meiro ꞌahine, vaze vetuḡazeadu danazoꞌi! Haḡai manoḡa vaze mazao haḡaoꞌi! Ḡaeꞌa ḡae bare niḡo mae ovoroꞌi! Roḡeru radoꞌi! Ago ḡarihe maḡunoꞌi!
Vazeꞌa zae mazao haḡai sauꞌa haḡaoꞌidene, ago maḡunoꞌi, ebu Zuhiꞌa boroꞌa zae sauꞌa rae modiroteꞌe teige zeḡe sauꞌa zuni rae modoꞌi!
Ebu haḡai manoḡa ꞌadi niduꞌa roꞌanoga ḡauḡaꞌe zamarone. Zaꞌe vaze teite zamarotitoꞌi! Zamarotitine, zae niduꞌa tibura onaiꞌuma.
Badiꞌaꞌa zaꞌe Keriso ahiri radu uniho manoḡano radifine huze nuꞌoziro. Eꞌanoꞌo Keriso zama roḡeḡaniꞌa zae zama ibitozenoꞌi! Ebu iḡaiḡa Badiꞌa mazao manoḡa tauḡi roꞌi!
Keriso ḡoere hina zamaze iriꞌvaꞌonoꞌi! Faifairu zamareꞌenaꞌa ihotitoꞌi ebu iradugutitoꞌi! Zae zamao Badiꞌa mazao manoḡa tauḡi radu, Salamo badaḡa, kuru badaḡa zu Vine Zaḡoḡaniꞌa ziniꞌeteꞌe badaḡa moꞌi!
Ebu nagini ḡoeroꞌidene, ga nagini haḡaoꞌidene, Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu niḡano ḡau niduꞌa haḡaoꞌi! Ebu ane niḡano Badiꞌa, emeḡe Mama mazao manoḡa tauḡi roꞌi!
Roḡae, ohozeze ḡoere egoꞌi, mazaḡa ꞌougine, Zuhiꞌa Boro moneo raꞌeteꞌe roḡaeḡaniꞌa haḡaiꞌuma haḡaiḡa haḡaeꞌohe.
Ohoze, inudeze zamaroꞌi, ebu ago sausau zoꞌi!
Tahiꞌa komeꞌa komeꞌa, zaꞌe iḡaiḡa viꞌu mogo ḡoere niduꞌa egoꞌi, mazaḡa zaꞌe ꞌouge haḡaine, Zuhiꞌa Boroꞌe matuꞌiꞌuma.
Nanu, mama, tahiꞌaze zamaze ago adufoꞌi! ꞌOugine, zamazeꞌa vetuḡaraꞌuma zu inarazeꞌa ovoiꞌuma.
Tuḡure azaḡa, ḡuꞌa teige gauꞌeteꞌe azaḡa, zae gau niduꞌa zamaḡano, zuhiꞌaze tuḡureze ego zenoꞌi! Zeꞌe raha ꞌada daꞌo zuhiꞌaziꞌe rehano, ego zenoꞌi! Ebu zuhiꞌazeꞌa horozadu matuꞌoga veize radu ago zamare gauoꞌi! Rehano, Zuhiꞌa Boro rihoneꞌenaꞌa zae zuhiꞌa veize hube hune gauoꞌi!
Ebu nagini gauḡa zae zuhiꞌa veize haḡaoꞌidene, zamaze niduꞌa hanadu Zuhiꞌa Boro veize gaueꞌeteꞌe teige haḡaoꞌi! Zaꞌe vaze veize daꞌo mene gaueꞌe rehano, Zuhiꞌa Boro veize borofe gaueꞌohe.
Mazaḡa ḡianoꞌi! Za edeḡa, Badiꞌa mone raꞌeteꞌe azaḡa ziniꞌuma reiroteꞌe ḡauḡaꞌe, zaeꞌa gaueꞌeteꞌe naeḡa haḡaeꞌohe radu, Zuhiꞌa Boroꞌa ziniꞌuma. Eꞌanoꞌo zaeꞌa ꞌouge zae zuhiꞌa veize haḡaeꞌetaꞌaꞌe, Zuhiꞌa Boro Keriso veize gaueꞌohe.
Ḡianoꞌi! Badiꞌaꞌe nize boro ga nize zuhuꞌa rehano, vazeꞌa haḡai sauꞌa haḡaetene, eꞌe naeḡa ziniꞌuma.
Zuhiꞌa azaḡa, zae tuḡure azaḡaꞌe haḡai duduḡano daꞌo zuhiꞌazoꞌi, ebu vaze nu daꞌo ago faizoꞌi, rehano niduꞌa faizoꞌi! Mazaḡa za mene ꞌougine, zae Zuhiꞌa, adureo radiuꞌeteꞌeꞌa, haḡaize ḡianadu eꞌe naeḡa ziniꞌuma.
Zaꞌe iḡaiḡa kurauꞌenoꞌi! Zamazeꞌe raꞌaneꞌenaꞌa bohanadu, Badiꞌa mazao manoḡa tauḡi raꞌenaꞌa kuranoꞌi!
Ebu emeḡe veize zuni kuranoꞌi, emeḡeꞌa Badiꞌa ḡoere haramiꞌuma ibiḡa aneꞌa haḡaifine. ꞌOugine, Keriso hariḡa Badiꞌaꞌa ane zamao ibite obonetiroteꞌe emeḡeꞌa harame fureniꞌuma. Eꞌe Keriso hariḡa harameꞌeteꞌe uꞌano ḡuꞌano ohohiro ꞌahine, za ꞌouge umizeꞌohe.
Ebu Badiꞌaꞌa gau ꞌadi iniroteꞌe idunaḡano Keriso hariḡa eḡeꞌa doḡoꞌani rae furenifine kuranoꞌi!
Mada manoḡa hidoꞌidene Keriso aḡuꞌa azaḡa danazoga veize faine zamare haḡaoꞌi!
Ebu zeḡe teite ḡoeroꞌidene, iḡaiḡa ḡoere iniga hina namize ḡorezoꞌi! ꞌOugine za ze teite ḡoretitine faine naenaeziꞌuma.
Eꞌe zae uꞌa Tukiko tuḡuneꞌohe. Aniꞌe emeḡe nego zu emeḡe zamarone. Ebu anie ekalesia azaḡa faifairu danazeꞌeteꞌe vazeḡa, zu Zuhiꞌa Boro tuḡure haḡaeꞌenaꞌa eḡe teite gaueꞌohe. Aniꞌe ꞌadama eḡeꞌa nouge nouge radiuꞌeteꞌe edemaziꞌuma, zaeꞌa eꞌe ederadu inarifine.
<range>
Onesimo zuni ani teite tuḡune amiꞌuma. Aniꞌe emeḡe nego zu emeḡe zamarone. Ebu aniꞌe hubehune Badiꞌa zamareꞌohe, zuni aniꞌe zae nabudi ꞌahoga. Zeꞌe emeḡeꞌa nouge nouge radiuꞌeteꞌe niduꞌa edemaziꞌuma.
Eḡe teite ḡuꞌano radiuꞌeteꞌe vazeḡa ꞌahoga, niḡa Arisitakoꞌa zae veize uhiu tuḡureꞌohe. Banabasi nabuga, Mareko zuni uhiu tuḡureꞌohe. Aneꞌa amiꞌuma ḡoeꞌa eḡeꞌa ibite tuḡuriro. Eꞌanoꞌo ani amoꞌidene, faine mae ḡihinoꞌi!
Vaze ꞌahoga niḡa Iesu, ane zuni uhiu tuḡureꞌohe. Niḡa ꞌahogaꞌe Iusto rae huneꞌohe. Badiꞌaꞌa vaze zama ibito zenoga veize eḡe teite gaueꞌeteꞌe azaḡa boꞌaḡano zeḡe uḡidu ahi daꞌoꞌe Iuda azaḡa. Ze iḡaiḡa eḡe danaheꞌetene zamaheꞌa matueꞌohe.
Zae nabudi ꞌahoga, Epafara, aniꞌe Keriso Iesu tuḡure vazeḡa. Ani zuni uhiu tuḡureꞌohe. Ani zae veize kurauꞌetene, iḡaiḡa inare kurauꞌohe, Badiꞌaꞌa zae mazao urateꞌeteꞌe ḡauḡa niduꞌa edere hauḡadu, edau gigaranoga veize.
Eꞌa ani horoninutene, aniꞌe hubehune zae ebu Laodikea zu Hierapoli neḡa azaḡa veize inare haḡueꞌohe.
Emeḡe nego zu emeḡe zamorone, doketa vazeḡa niḡa Luka ebu Demaꞌa uhiu tuḡureꞌohe.
Izidi eḡeꞌa uhiu tuḡureꞌeteꞌe ḡoeꞌa Laodikea neḡano Badiꞌa mone raꞌeteꞌe azaḡa zenoꞌi ebu roḡae ꞌahoga, niḡa Numufa zu ane neo kurauꞌeteꞌe azaḡa veize zuni zenoꞌi.
Fefa ꞌadi vaze ꞌahoganiꞌa zae mazao meꞌode hauḡoꞌidene, hena, Laodikea ekalesiaḡa veize tuḡuroꞌi, zeḡe kuru neḡano meꞌode furenoga. Ebu zaꞌe, hena, Laodikea ekalesia veize eḡeꞌa tuḡuriroteꞌe fefaḡa madu meꞌodoꞌi!
Ebu Arekipo ninaꞌa, “Zuhiꞌa Boroꞌa haroteꞌe gauḡa haḡae hauḡoꞌi!”, rae noꞌi!
Eḡe Pauloꞌa uhiu ḡoeꞌa ꞌadi eḡe ꞌevore hina mirineꞌohe. Eḡeꞌa Keriso hari manoḡa uꞌano ḡuꞌano radiuꞌeteꞌe zamaroꞌi, ebu kuranoꞌi! Badiꞌa manohuganiꞌa zae teite radiuꞌenoꞌi!
Eḡe, Paulo zu Silasi ebu Timoteoꞌa Tesalonika habaꞌa ekalesiaḡa azaḡa veize fefa ꞌadi miriheꞌohe. Zaꞌe Badiꞌa emeḡe Mama zu Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Keriso moneo raꞌeteꞌe azaḡa. Eme ꞌahige rae zihi: Badiꞌaꞌa manoḡa zu zama roḡeḡa ziniꞌenoꞌi!
Emeḡe kuru zamaḡano, zae veize kurauꞌetene, eme zae uꞌano Badiꞌa mazao iḡaiḡa manoḡa tauḡi raꞌohe.
Mazaḡa emeḡeꞌa, Badiꞌa emeḡe Mama mazao kurauꞌetene, iḡaiḡa zae zamareꞌenaꞌa, ꞌahige raꞌohe: Zaꞌe Badiꞌa mazao fieꞌenaꞌa, gaueꞌohe. Ebu zae zamarone vaze mazaoꞌe boro ꞌahine, zaꞌe zeḡe veize gau boro haḡaeꞌohe. Ebu Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Kerisoꞌa hube hune bare onaiꞌuma raꞌeteꞌe ḡoeꞌa mae obene giganeꞌohe.
Nego nabudi, Badiꞌa zamarone azaḡa, eme edeḡa, za ꞌai Badiꞌaꞌa ohotiro.
Emeḡeꞌa hari manoḡa haramo zinirotene, mene ḡoere isoḡa hina rehano, inaraḡeita haramido. Eꞌe zamaḡano Vine Zaḡoḡaniꞌa zae mazao gauadu, emeḡeꞌa haramidotaꞌaꞌe hube hune huga rae ihozido. Zu zae zuni edeḡa emeḡeꞌa zae teite radiunuteꞌe zamaḡano, nouge nouge zae danazinutaꞌe. Zaeꞌa emeḡe radoneo horonidotene, hari manoḡaꞌe mene ḡuriro hariḡa reido.
Zaꞌe hari manoḡa mae ḡihinirotene, aduga boro hidiro. Rehano, Vine Zaḡoḡaniꞌa matuꞌu hina iriꞌavoziro ꞌahine, za matuꞌuzeta hari manoḡa mae ḡihine onainu. Zaꞌa ꞌouginutaꞌaꞌe, emeḡe haḡai zuni Zuhiꞌa Boro haḡai haḡaiḡano onainu.
Eꞌanoꞌo Makedonia zu Akaia habaꞌano radiuꞌeteꞌe ekalesiaḡa azaḡaniꞌa zaeꞌa haḡaeꞌeteꞌe haḡaiḡa hariḡa egaduni, zae haḡaio haḡae onamiꞌuma raꞌohe.
Mazaḡa Zuhiꞌa Boro hari manoḡaniꞌa zae mazaonoꞌo bororanadu, mene Makedonia zu Akaia habaꞌano daꞌo rehano, haba ꞌahoga ꞌahoga zamaḡano zuni bororu onaeha. Ebu zaeꞌa Badiꞌa mazao fieꞌeteꞌe hariḡa vaze niduꞌa igi hauḡeha. Eꞌanoꞌo emeꞌe zae hariꞌe mene bare reꞌuma.
Mazaḡa vaze niduꞌa edeḡa, zeꞌe, emeḡeꞌa Tesalonika habaꞌano hari manoḡa haramadu, zaeꞌa mae ḡihiniroteꞌe, eꞌe hariḡa meꞌodofiꞌohe. Ebu zaeꞌa nouge nouge ḡuriro badiꞌaḡa higone modadu, hube hune radiuꞌeteꞌe Badiꞌaḡa daꞌo zae Zuhiꞌa Boro radu, tuḡureḡa haḡaeꞌeteꞌe, eꞌe hariḡa zuni meꞌodofiꞌohe.
Ebu zaꞌe Theovaiteꞌe guhineꞌohe, rae meꞌodofiꞌohe. Aꞌe Iesu, Badiꞌaꞌa runeonoꞌo bare ḡaboniroteꞌe vazeḡa, zuni mada ḡonagano haḡai sauꞌa uꞌano Badiꞌaꞌa aduga ziniꞌuma madaḡano, ani eme ḡabofiꞌuma vazeḡa.
Nego nabudi, za edeḡa, emeḡeꞌa Tesalonika neḡano ꞌiꞌudirotaꞌaꞌe, mene tauḡe amiro. Mazaḡa zae ḡehaḡa huneꞌa eꞌea hari manoḡa mae ḡihiniro.
Za edeḡa, emeḡeꞌa zae ne ꞌizema amogano, Filipi neḡano vazeꞌa ifi sausaufiro, zuni rae aduga rifiro. Rehano Tesalonika neḡa amirotene, emeḡe Badiꞌaꞌa inarafeadu, agire boꞌaḡano, rehano Badiꞌa hari manoḡa inare haramiro.
Mazaḡa emeḡeꞌa haramirotaꞌaꞌe, zae tutuze veꞌozifine ga, haḡai sauꞌa zae mazao haḡaifine zu zae soꞌozifine mene haramiro.
Rehano emeꞌe hari manoḡa harameꞌohe, mazaḡa Badiꞌaꞌa eme ꞌai manoḡa radu, hari manoḡa haramiꞌuma gauḡano ohofiro ꞌahine. Eꞌanoꞌo emeḡeꞌa harameꞌetene, mene vazeꞌa matuꞌoga, rehano Badiꞌaꞌa matuꞌiꞌuma ibiḡano harameꞌohe. Badiꞌa ani emeḡe zama faifaine ḡianeꞌeteꞌe vazeḡa.
Zae edeḡa, emeḡeꞌa ḡorezinutaꞌe mene zamaze anoga radu, ga zae mazao ḡau mouga radu mene soꞌe ḡorezinu. Badiꞌa huga ani eme haḡai edeḡa.
Zuni emeꞌe, mene zaeꞌa ga vaze ꞌahoga ꞌahoganiꞌa nife mae ḡihinoga radu gauido,
emeꞌe Kerisoꞌa tuḡuiroteꞌe apostoloḡa azaḡa ꞌahine, nife boro azaḡa rouga zuni idaḡa. Rehano emeꞌe, roḡaꞌeꞌa ubuga duḡuru faifaizeꞌeteꞌe teige, zae boꞌaḡano roḡeru radiunu.
Eme zae zamare borofiro ꞌahine, matuꞌufeta Badiꞌa hari manoḡa haramo zinirotene, ḡabonefe niduꞌa hina zae danazoga veize ḡau niduꞌa haḡao ziniro. Mazaḡa emeḡe zamarone zae mazaoꞌe boro bagaḡa.
Nego nabudi, za hubehune edeḡa, emeḡeꞌa zae mazao Badiꞌa hari manoḡa haraminuteꞌe zamaḡano, emeḡeꞌa inare hune gauinutaꞌaꞌe. Emeꞌe zaeꞌa emeḡe uꞌano hadize mene modifine, madai zu ohere niduꞌa gauido.
Hubehune zaꞌe haḡaife horoniro, ebu Badiꞌa ane zuni edeḡa. Zaꞌe, Badiꞌa mazao fieꞌeteꞌe azaḡa teite, emeḡeꞌa radiunuteꞌe madaḡano, haḡaifeꞌe, Badiꞌaꞌa matuꞌiꞌuma haḡaiḡa zu duduḡa ebu mene veꞌoḡa haḡaiḡa haḡainu.
Zae edeḡa, ohozeꞌa ubuga duḡuru ihozeꞌeteꞌe teige, eme zae zaeꞌa fie gigaru onamogaradu danazinu, zu inara zinido, ebu iraduguzido, Badiꞌaꞌa matuꞌiꞌuma haḡaiḡano radiu onamifine. Mazaḡa za Badiꞌaꞌa huzeꞌohe, aneꞌa zae faifaine zuhiꞌaziꞌuma.
<range>
Zuni eme zae uꞌano iḡaiḡa Badiꞌa mazao manoḡa tauḡi raꞌohe, mazaḡa za aḡua mazaḡano emeḡeꞌa Badiꞌa hari manoḡa haramo zinirotaꞌaꞌe mene vaze ḡoere, rehano Badiꞌa ḡoere rae radu zaeꞌa mae ḡihiniro. Aꞌe hube Badiꞌa ḡoere. Ebu eꞌe ḡoeꞌaniꞌe, zae, Badiꞌa ḡoere mae ḡihineꞌeteꞌe azaḡa, zamao gaueꞌohe.
Eꞌanoꞌo, nego nabudi, zaꞌe Iudea habaꞌa zamaḡano Keriso Iesu niḡano radiuꞌeteꞌe ekalesiaḡa azaḡaniꞌa haḡaidoteꞌe teige haḡairo. Zeḡeꞌa Iuda azaḡa mazaonoꞌo aduga hididoteꞌe teige, zae zuni haba tiba azaḡa mazaonoꞌo aduga hidido.
Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu ebu peroveta azaḡa runedirotaꞌaꞌe, Iuda azaḡaniꞌa, ebu emeḡe hegofe bufirotaꞌa zuni Iuda azaḡaniꞌa. Zeꞌe Badiꞌaꞌa mene matuꞌiꞌuma haḡaiḡa haḡaeꞌohe. Zeꞌe vaze niduꞌa agire.
Iuda azaḡaꞌe, mene Iuda azaḡa mazao hari manoḡa haramoga mene uratadu, eme garareꞌohe. Hena, zeꞌa ḡabone hidiꞌuma radu. Deꞌugeꞌenaꞌa, zeḡe haḡai sauꞌa ragate ragate tiꞌohe. Eꞌanoꞌo Badiꞌaꞌa maḡuno zenadu, naeḡa haḡaoga raꞌohe.
Nego nabudi, Tesalonika neḡano Iuda azaḡaniꞌa aduga boro fureraroteꞌe uꞌano, zaꞌe munemune azaḡa teiḡe emeḡeꞌa muhize iḡuniro, onao izidi mada nu vitineha (Aꞌe ahirioꞌe mene ḡiazeꞌe rehano, zamafeꞌe zae zamareꞌohe). Ebu zae ḡiazoga urate rudaunu ꞌahine, zae vaḡe bare amoga radu ibi vaḡe onainu.
Oꞌe, eme zae vaḡe amihi reiro. Hubehune eḡe, Pauloꞌa bare bare ibiḡa vaḡiro rehano, Sataniꞌa haḡai nunuoꞌnoꞌo ꞌuiro.
Eme uraꞌe bare ḡiazihi raꞌohe. Mazaḡa emeḡeꞌa zamareꞌetene, zaꞌe hubehune Badiꞌa mazao fie gigaruꞌeꞌuma, onamo emeḡe Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesuꞌa bare onaiteꞌe madaḡano ane zamao edaꞌuma. Ebu eꞌe madaḡano emeꞌe zaeꞌa naeḡa meiteꞌe uꞌano niguziꞌuma, ebu zae uꞌano matuꞌiꞌuma.
Hubehune eme zaꞌe niguzeꞌohe, ebu zae uꞌano matuꞌeꞌohe.
Eme ꞌouge guhiu onamoga mene idararotene, eme raenaꞌa, Timoteoꞌe zae vaḡe tuḡune amiꞌuma, ebu emeꞌe emeḡe daꞌo Atena neḡano radiꞌuma reiro. Timoteoꞌe, emeḡe nego, emeḡe teite Badiꞌa gau haḡaeꞌohe, ebu Keriso hari manoḡa harameꞌohe. Eꞌanoꞌo eme Timoteo tuḡuniro, aniꞌe zaeꞌa Badiꞌa mazao fie gigaranoga veize danaziuma.
<range>
ꞌOugine zaeꞌa aduga hidine, zamazeꞌe mene hagariꞌuma. Mazaḡa zae zaeꞌe edeḡa, Keriso mazao fieꞌeteꞌe azaḡaniꞌe aduga hidiꞌuma.
Eme zae teite radiudoteꞌe zamaḡano, emeḡe niduꞌa nariga aduga hideꞌohe rae, bare bare iraduguzido. ebu zae edeḡa, eꞌe haḡaiḡaniꞌe zae mazao fureraro.
Eꞌanoꞌo eꞌa guhiu onamoga mene idararotene, zaeꞌa nouge nouge Keriso mazao fieꞌeteꞌe ederoga veize Timoteo tuḡuniro. Mazaḡa eꞌa riharotaꞌaꞌe, Sataniꞌa ibi nunuo soꞌozadu zaeꞌa Keriso mazao fieꞌeteꞌeꞌa dauḡiꞌuma reiro. ꞌOugine, emeḡeꞌa zae veize gaue onairotaꞌaꞌe, huga oꞌoꞌa reꞌuma.
Rehano Timoteo ani izidi zae mazaonoꞌo bare onaeha, ebu zae hari manoḡa odohe onaeha, raenaꞌa, zaꞌe Badiꞌa mazao ize fieꞌohe, zuni Badiꞌa zu vaze zamareꞌohe. Ebu zaꞌe iḡaiḡa eme zamareꞌohe, ebu emeḡeꞌa ḡiaze hunihi raꞌeteꞌe teige, zae zuni ḡiafe hunihi raꞌohe.
Eꞌanoꞌo nego nabudi, emeꞌe ꞌahama aduga boro hideꞌe rehano, zaꞌe ize Keriso mazao fieꞌohe rae egatene, zamafe inaraneha.
Ebu izidi emeḡeꞌa matuꞌufeta radiuꞌohe, mazaḡa zaꞌe Zuhiꞌa Boro mazao edau gigaruꞌe ꞌahine.
Mazaḡa zaeꞌa Keriso mazao ize fieꞌeteꞌe haḡaiḡaniꞌa matuꞌofiꞌohe, eme kurauꞌetene, zae uꞌano Badiꞌa mazao nouge nouge manoḡa tauḡi reꞌuma?
Mada niduꞌa ohere niduꞌa, zamafe niduꞌa hina kurauꞌohe, emeḡe zae teite bare hidoga, zu bare ihozoga, zae Keriso mazao arane fie gigarafine.
ꞌOugadu eme ꞌahige kurauꞌohe: Badiꞌa, emeḡe Mamaꞌa, zu emeḡe Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesuꞌa, emeḡeꞌa zae vaḡe amiteꞌe ibiḡa mae bohanifine!
Ebu Zuhiꞌa Boroꞌa zae zamarone borofadu, vaze niduꞌa zamaroga, zuni zae zamarotitoga, emeḡeꞌa zae zamareꞌeteꞌe teige.
Ebu eme ꞌadige kurauꞌohe: Kerisoꞌa zamaze inare radoga, Badiꞌa emeḡe Mama zamao haḡaize deheḡa reifine, zu sauꞌa moneo mene debazifine, aꞌe Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesuꞌa ane moneo raꞌeteꞌe azaḡa teite bare onaiteꞌe madaḡano.
Eꞌanoꞌo nego nabudi, eme Badiꞌaꞌa matuꞌiꞌuma radoneḡa ibiḡa ihozido. Ebu izidi zaꞌe eꞌe radoneḡano radiuꞌohe. Rehano eme Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu niḡano rinede umizeꞌohe. Mazaḡa Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesuꞌa rifiroteꞌe ḡoeꞌa emeḡeꞌa ihozidotaꞌaꞌe zae edeḡa, za eꞌe ibiḡano daꞌo radiu onameꞌenoꞌi!
<range>
Badiꞌa ani uraꞌe, zaeꞌa zaḡozaḡoga urateꞌohe, mazaḡa zaꞌe Badiꞌaꞌa mae avo tiro ꞌahine. Zaꞌe daro haḡaiḡaonoꞌo vaginoi!
Ebu ohoze ohoze, zaꞌe zaḡozaḡe zu gubane ibiḡano ꞌahirize tuḡaneꞌenaꞌa, dugunoꞌi!
U ubuma gezo radoneḡano ago radoꞌi! Aꞌe Badiꞌa aḡuꞌa azaḡa haḡai.
Eꞌe haḡaiḡa sauꞌaꞌe negoḡo nabugo mazao ago haḡaoꞌi! Inuga teite ago darooꞌi! Mazaḡa ꞌuguḡa haḡaiḡa haḡaeꞌeteꞌe vazeḡaꞌe Zuhiꞌa Boroꞌa eꞌe naeḡa haꞌuma. ꞌAdiꞌe emeḡeꞌa ibiteo ꞌoma irina riḡa zi edemazidoteꞌe ḡoeꞌa.
Badiꞌaꞌa emeḡe zamafirotaꞌaꞌe, daro haḡaiḡa mene haḡaifine, rehano zaḡozaḡo radoneḡano radifine.
Eꞌanoꞌo iradugu ḡoeꞌa ꞌadi mene mae ḡihiniꞌuma vazeḡaꞌe, mene vaze iradugu ḡoeꞌa mae ḡihineꞌohe. Rehano, Badiꞌa, ani ane Vine Zaḡoḡa tuḡuno zenadu, danazeꞌe rehano, iradugu ḡoeꞌa rae modeꞌohe.
U nego nabudi teite zamarotiteꞌeteꞌe moneoꞌe, za ꞌai Badiꞌaꞌa ihozadu, zamarotiteꞌohe. Eꞌanoꞌo mene miriho ziniꞌuma.
Hubehune zaꞌe Makedonia habaꞌa niduꞌa zamaḡano Iesu mone raꞌeteꞌe azaḡa niduꞌa zamareꞌohe. Rehano nego nabudi, eme bare umizihi! Bare bare ꞌougeꞌenoꞌi!
Ebu ꞌadiꞌe, emeḡeꞌa zae teite radiunuteꞌe madaḡano, ihozidoteꞌe ḡoeꞌa rehano, bare ziꞌohe. Zamaze rinedeꞌenaꞌa, imuimuꞌuhi radiuꞌenoꞌi! Ebu evoreze hina zae zae gau daꞌo zamare haḡaeꞌenoꞌi! Vaze ago dudizeꞌenoꞌi!
ꞌOugine, Iesu mone mene raꞌeteꞌe azaḡaniꞌa zae radone horonadu, gubaziꞌuma. Zuni zae inarao gaueꞌenoꞌi, zaeꞌa ogomu, dabua, radone ḡauḡa niduꞌa meifine! ꞌOugine, zaꞌe vaze ꞌahoganiꞌa mene fereziꞌuma.
Nego nabudi, eme uraꞌe zaeꞌa ederoga, Iesu ni mae ḡihineꞌeteꞌe azaḡaniꞌa rudaroteꞌe mazao naginiꞌa fureraꞌumaꞌe. Badiꞌa aḡuꞌa azaḡa rudaꞌuma teige, zaꞌe zamaze ago vetuḡa ranoꞌi! Ze ꞌane rune vazeḡaꞌe mene bare ḡabodiꞌuma raꞌohe.
Eme, ḡoere ꞌadiꞌe huga raꞌohe. Iesu ani rudaro, ebu bare ḡabodiro. Eꞌanoꞌo Iesu ni mae ḡihinadu, rudaroteꞌe azaḡaꞌe, Iesuꞌa bare ovaiꞌuma madaḡano, Badiꞌaꞌa Iesu teite bare zamaziꞌuma.
Emeḡeꞌa ꞌada ziꞌeteꞌe ḡoeꞌaꞌe, Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesuꞌa reiroteꞌe ḡoeꞌa. Eme, ize ḡaboga radiuꞌeteꞌe azaḡaꞌe ize radiu onamo, Zuhiꞌa Boroꞌa bare ovaineꞌe, rudaroteꞌe azaḡaꞌe ibite ḡaboziꞌuma. Eꞌe enoganobuꞌu emeḡe zamafiꞌuma.
Zuhiꞌa Boro aneꞌa rune azaḡa iḡunoi raenaꞌa ḡihau huaune, tuḡure viga ḡihiꞌaniꞌa huaꞌuma, ebu kibi hodoga igiꞌuma. Eꞌe zamaḡano, Zuhiꞌa Boro aneꞌa adureonoꞌo ovaiꞌuma. Ebu Keriso mazao fiadu rudaroteꞌe azaḡaniꞌa gezo ḡabode iḡuniꞌuma.
Eꞌe enogano, eme, ize ḡaboga radiuꞌeteꞌe azaḡaꞌe, Badiꞌaꞌa zeḡe teite idaḡa mae ḡihifiꞌuma, ebu magube zamaḡa diuḡiꞌuma, adureo Zuhiꞌa Boro teite hidoga veize. Ebu emeꞌe Zuhiꞌa Boro teite radiu tuḡutuḡu radiꞌuma.
Zaꞌe, eḡeꞌa ꞌada teateꞌe ḡoeꞌa hina zae bare inaratitoꞌi!
Nego nabudi, Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesuꞌa bare onaiꞌuma madaḡaꞌe ꞌahama mene miriho ziniꞌuma,
mazaḡa za edeḡa tauḡi, Zuhiꞌa Boroꞌa bare onaiꞌuma madaḡaꞌe. Ḡonoreꞌa ohere onaiteꞌe teige onaiꞌuma, ebu vaze niduꞌa zaguzagaꞌuma.
Vaze vazeꞌa raenaꞌa, “Eme uniho manoḡa maha, ebu aduga ꞌahoga oꞌoꞌa.” rae reꞌoreꞌeꞌeteꞌe zamaḡano, sauꞌa boroꞌa tabatabaze feuradu, zaguzaguziꞌuma. Aꞌe roḡae ahiꞌetaniꞌa ene furenoga radu, gigiꞌaniꞌa tabatabane feurohuꞌeteꞌe teige fureraꞌuma. Ebu zeꞌe eꞌe aduḡa boroꞌa fureruꞌeteꞌe mode feranoga mene idaḡa.
Rehano nego nabudi, zaꞌe mene uzaboo radiuꞌeteꞌe azaḡa. Eꞌanoꞌo Iesuꞌa bare ovaine, ḡonoreꞌa zaguzaguzeꞌeteꞌe teige, mene zaguzaguziꞌuma.
Zaꞌe niduꞌa madai zu agaḡa zamaḡano radiuꞌeteꞌe azaḡa. Emetaꞌe ohere zu uzabo zamaḡano mene radiuꞌeteꞌe azaḡa.
Eꞌanoꞌo Iesuꞌe mene bare onaiꞌuma rae zamareꞌeteꞌe azaḡa teige, mene reꞌoreꞌe radiꞌuma! Ebu tohutohe radiꞌuma, zu haḡaife daꞌo faifaine duguniꞌuma.
Mazaḡa reꞌoreꞌe radiuꞌeteꞌe azaḡaꞌe uzabo zamaḡano reꞌoreꞌeꞌohe, ebu gage baboruꞌeteꞌe azaḡaꞌe uzabo zamaḡano gage baboruꞌohe.
Rehano emeꞌe madai agaḡano radiuꞌe ꞌahine, haḡaife daꞌo faifaine duguniꞌuma. Eꞌe haḡaiḡaꞌe eme ꞌahige haḡaiꞌuma: Badiꞌa mazao fiꞌuma, ebu Badiꞌa zu vaze zamariꞌuma. Aꞌe uti vazeḡaniꞌa ahiri biriḡa hina ahiꞌa ꞌueꞌeteꞌe heuḡa. Ebu eme Iesuꞌa bare onaadu ḡabofiꞌuma rae zamare gigaruꞌeꞌuma. Aꞌe uti vazeḡaniꞌa utio vadini biriḡa hina vadiga ꞌueꞌeteꞌe heuḡa.
Mazaḡa Badiꞌaꞌa emeḡe meꞌofirotaꞌaꞌe, mene maḡunofeadu, emeḡe sauꞌa naeḡa rififine, rehano Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Keriso tuḡunadu, emeḡe sauꞌa naeḡa mae vaḡinadu, ḡabofifine.
Aneꞌa onaiteꞌe madaḡano, emeꞌe ruga ga ḡaboga rehano, ane teite ḡabone tuḡutuḡu radoga veize, ani emeḡe veize rudaro.
Eꞌanoꞌo zae zaeꞌa eḡe ḡoere ꞌadi hina inaratitoꞌi, ebu Badiꞌa mazao fie gigarafine danatitoꞌi! Eꞌe haḡaiḡaꞌe zaeꞌa haḡae onaeha. Zaeꞌa ꞌouge daꞌo haḡaeꞌenoꞌi!
Nego nabudi, eme umizeꞌohe. Zae boꞌaḡano, Zuhiꞌa Boro ibi moneo gau boro haḡaiꞌenaꞌa ibitoziniꞌeteꞌe ebu iraduguzeꞌeteꞌe azaḡa gubazoꞌi!
Zeḡeꞌa zae veize gaueꞌeteꞌe haḡaiḡa uꞌano zamaze niduꞌa hina gubazoꞌi, ebu zamarone boro zeḡe mazao toꞌi! Zae zae niduꞌa uniho manoḡa zamaḡano radoꞌi!
Nego nabudi, eme umizeꞌohe. Gauoga mene urateꞌeteꞌe tubuḡa azaḡaꞌe zeḡe hadi gauḡa veize iraduguzoꞌi! Zamaḡa rereḡa azaḡaꞌe inarazoꞌi! Zoreḡa azaḡaꞌe danazoꞌi! Vaze niduꞌa mazao zamaze rinedoꞌi!
ꞌAhoganiꞌa ꞌahoga mazao sauꞌa haḡaoꞌidene, sausaunateꞌe vazeḡa ninaꞌa, eꞌe naeḡa ago haḡaoꞌi, rae noꞌi! Rehano iḡaiḡa nabugota zuni vaze niduꞌa mazao haḡai manoḡa daꞌo haḡaeꞌenoꞌi!
Zaꞌe Keriso moneo radiuꞌeteꞌe azaḡa, eꞌanoꞌo Badiꞌaꞌa zae mazaonoꞌo urateꞌeteꞌe haḡaiḡaꞌe ahiꞌe; Mada niduꞌa matuꞌe radiuꞌenoꞌi! Iḡaiḡa kurauꞌenoꞌi! Naginiꞌa fureranoꞌidene, sauꞌa manoḡa rehano, Badiꞌa mazao manoḡa tauḡi roꞌi!
<range>
<range>
Vine Zaḡoḡaniꞌa zae mazao gaueꞌeteꞌe ibiḡa ago ꞌuoꞌi!
Vine Zaḡoḡaniꞌa ziniꞌeteꞌe ḡoeꞌaꞌe huga ꞌoꞌoꞌa radu ago reꞌoreꞌone modoꞌi!
ꞌUguḡa ḡoeꞌa egoꞌidene, faine ḡianoꞌi! Ebu manoḡa ḡauḡaꞌe moꞌi,
u sauꞌa ḡauḡaꞌe ago moꞌi!
Eme ꞌahige kuratihi: Zama roḡeḡa rifeꞌeteꞌe Badiꞌaḡa, aneꞌa ane teige deheze huneꞌenaꞌa matuoziniꞌuma, ebu zaeꞌa haḡai sauꞌa mene haḡaoga veize, Badiꞌaꞌa vineze zu ahirize dananeꞌenoꞌi! Onamo, Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Kerisoꞌa bare onaiꞌuma.
Zae meꞌofiroteꞌe Badiꞌaḡa, ani ḡoereꞌe hugeita. Eꞌanoꞌo aneꞌa haḡao ziniꞌuma.
Nego nabudi, emeḡe veize kurauꞌenoꞌi!
Ebu zaꞌe, nego nabudi niduꞌa teite zama manoḡa teite mae ḡihitetoꞌi!
Zuhiꞌa Boro niḡano ziꞌohe. Fefa ꞌadiꞌe nego nabudi niduꞌa veize meꞌodoꞌi, zeḡe egoga veize!
Emeḡe Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Keriso ane manoḡaniꞌa zae mazao radiuꞌenoꞌi!
Eḡe, Paulo zu Silasi ebu Timoteoꞌa Tesalonika neḡa ekalesiaḡa azaḡa veize fefa ꞌadi miriheꞌohe. Zaꞌe, Badiꞌa emeḡe Mama zu Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Keriso moneo raꞌeteꞌe azaḡa.
Eme ꞌahige rae zihi: Badiꞌa emeḡe Mama zu Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Kerisoꞌa manoḡa zu zama roḡeḡa ziniꞌenoꞌi!
Nego nabudi, eme zae uꞌano iḡaiḡa Badiꞌa mazao manoḡa tauḡi raꞌohe. Eme ꞌouge haḡaeꞌetaꞌaꞌe manoḡa. Mazaḡa zaꞌa Badiꞌa mazao fieꞌetaꞌaꞌe bororu onameꞌohe, ebu zaꞌa zamarotiteꞌetaꞌa zuni bororuꞌohe.
Eꞌanoꞌo neḡa neḡano Badiꞌa mazao fieꞌeteꞌe ekalesiaḡa azaḡa mazao, harize meꞌodeꞌenaꞌa niguzeꞌohe. Zaeꞌa, Badiꞌa mazao fieꞌeteꞌe uꞌano, vazeꞌa agireziꞌeteꞌe, zu aduga boro zamaḡano, rehano zaꞌe zamaze oboneteadu Badiꞌa mazao fie gigaruꞌohe, rae ziꞌohe.
ꞌUguḡa haḡaiḡaniꞌa zae mazao fureruꞌetaꞌaꞌe, Badiꞌaꞌa mada ḡonagano ane ane haḡai naeḡa idane ziniꞌuma. Ebu Badiꞌaꞌa ibitofieteꞌe haba'a diuḡogaꞌe idaḡa rae reꞌuma veize, zaꞌe aduga madaḡano ꞌouge edau gigaraunu.
Badiꞌaꞌa haḡaeꞌeteꞌe haḡaiḡaꞌe niduꞌa duduḡa. Eꞌanoꞌo zae sausauzeꞌeteꞌe azaḡaꞌe Badiꞌaꞌa eꞌe naeḡa ziniꞌuma,
u zae, aduga hideꞌeteꞌe azaḡaꞌe, Badiꞌaꞌa ahiri oheneꞌeteꞌe manoḡa ziniꞌuma, ebu emeḡe zuni rifiꞌuma. Eꞌe haḡaiḡaꞌe, Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesuꞌa inara aneruḡa ḡehaḡa teite zu ire roga duhuḡa teite adureonoꞌo fureraꞌuma madaḡano, Badiꞌaꞌa haḡaiꞌuma.
Badiꞌa ni mae ḡihinoga mene urateꞌeteꞌe azaḡa zu, emeḡe Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu hari manoḡa igi modeꞌeteꞌe azaḡaꞌe, Badiꞌaꞌa eꞌe sauꞌaḡa naeḡa ziniꞌuma.
Eꞌe naeḡaꞌe radiu tuḡutuḡu gigiꞌaḡa ziniꞌuma. Zeꞌe Zuhiꞌa Boro radone habaꞌanonoꞌo enoziꞌuma, zuni ane inaraḡa boro bagaḡaonoꞌo mae vaḡiziꞌuma.
Eꞌe haḡaiḡaꞌe Zuhiꞌa Boroꞌa bare onaiꞌuma madaḡano fureraꞌuma. Ebu Badiꞌa mone raꞌeteꞌe azaḡaniꞌa Zuhiꞌa Boro niguniꞌuma, ebu Iesu ni mae ḡihiniroteꞌe azaḡaꞌe ane agaḡa horonadu zaguzagaꞌuma. Zaꞌe emeḡeꞌa Iesu hariḡa meꞌodo ziniroteꞌe mae ḡihiniro ꞌahine, zae zuni zeḡe teite eꞌea radiuꞌenaꞌa Zuhiꞌa Boro horoniꞌuma.
Eꞌanoꞌo eme eꞌe zamaradu, zae veize iḡaiḡa kurauꞌohe, Badiꞌa ani ꞌahige rae rouga veize: Zaꞌe ane ibio radiuꞌetaꞌaꞌe idaḡa ra reifine. Ebu aneꞌa inaraḡa zenadu, zaeꞌa haḡai manoḡa niduꞌa haḡaihi raꞌeteꞌe, zu Badiꞌa mazao fieꞌeteꞌe uꞌano haḡai manoḡa niduꞌa haḡaoꞌi!
Emeḡeꞌa ꞌouge kurauꞌetaꞌaꞌe, emeḡe Badiꞌa zu Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Kerisoꞌa manoḡa ziniꞌeteꞌe uꞌano, vaze vazeꞌa zae haḡai manoḡa horonadu, emeḡe Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu nigunifine, zu zae haḡai uꞌano zae zuni Iesuꞌa niguzifine.
Nego nabudi, emeḡe Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesuꞌa bare onaiteꞌe zu emeḡe nuꞌofadu Iesu teite hidiꞌuma moneo ꞌahige ziꞌohe:
Zuhiꞌa Boroꞌa onaiꞌuma madaḡa ꞌai feureha reiteꞌe ḡoeꞌa egoꞌidene, zamaze ago koukouroꞌi zu ago adunoꞌi! Vaze ꞌahoganiꞌa Vine Zaḡoḡaniꞌa eꞌe ḡoeꞌaꞌe rae inare reiteꞌe ga, vazeꞌa haramiroteꞌe ga, emeḡeꞌa tuḡuriroteꞌe fefaḡa zamaḡano touga rae reiteꞌe zuni ago egoꞌi!
Zaꞌe eꞌeguḡa ḡuriroḡa ḡoeꞌaꞌe ago hune zu egoꞌi! Mazaḡa Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesuꞌa ize ꞌizema onaogano, ibite ize vaze ḡehaḡaniꞌa Badiꞌa aḡireniꞌuma, ebu Badiꞌa goro ḡoeꞌa rae modeꞌeteꞌe vazeḡa sauꞌa huneḡaniꞌa fureraꞌuma. Aniꞌe ḡonagano Badiꞌaꞌa ire rogao mae feuniꞌuma.
Aniꞌe Badiꞌa huga, ebu vazeꞌa Badiꞌa teiḡe kurauꞌeteꞌe ḡauḡa niduꞌa agireniꞌuma, ebu Badiꞌa zu ḡau niduꞌa vitinadu, aneꞌa ane mae hitananiꞌuma. Ebu aniꞌe Badiꞌa Neo diuḡe ehoriꞌuma, ebu aneꞌa ane bare ‘Eꞌe Badiꞌa huga’ rae reꞌuma.
Zae edeḡa, ḡoere ꞌadiꞌe eḡeꞌa zae teite radiudoteꞌe madaḡano zido.
Zuni zae edeḡa, izidi aḡire vazeḡaniꞌa fureraꞌuma ibiḡa naginiꞌa ꞌueꞌetaꞌaꞌe. Badiꞌaꞌa ḡoitoriroteꞌe madaḡanobuꞌu, aniꞌa fureraꞌuma.
Badiꞌa goro ḡoeꞌa aḡirohauꞌeteꞌe zamaroneḡa sauꞌaniꞌa vaze vaze zamao sifu gaueꞌohe, rehano hunioꞌe mene fufurimaꞌuma. Mazaḡa aḡire vazeḡaniꞌa gauiꞌuma ibiḡaꞌe vaze ꞌahoganiꞌa ꞌue radiꞌuma, aḡire vazeḡa ꞌue radiuetaꞌaꞌe vazeḡaꞌe Badiꞌaꞌa mae vaḡiniꞌuduꞌu,
aniꞌa fureraꞌuma. Aniꞌe madaḡa meine, Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesuꞌa ḡoeꞌa inaraḡa hina sausaune runiꞌuma, ebu Iesuꞌa onaiteꞌe agaḡaḡa boro hina sausaune runiꞌuma.
Aḡire vazeḡaꞌe Sataniꞌa gauiꞌuma ibiḡano gaue onaiꞌuma. Sataniꞌa gigiꞌaḡa hanadu aniꞌe haḡai nu badeḡa, tahi zu zaguzagaꞌuma haḡaiḡa ebu haḡai nunu niduꞌa ḡuriro moneo haḡaiꞌuma.
Ebu aḡire vazeḡa sauꞌa haḡaiḡa nunu niduꞌa hina rune ibiḡano radiuꞌeteꞌe azaḡa soꞌoziꞌuma. Zeꞌe Badiꞌa hari manoḡa, ḡoere huga mae ḡihinifone, Badiꞌaꞌa ḡabozifo rehano, zeꞌe mae ḡihinoga mene uratiro. Eꞌanoꞌo ze mazaoꞌe rune ibiḡano onamoga daꞌo.
Zeꞌe Badiꞌa hari manoḡa mene mae ḡihiniro ahine, Badiꞌaꞌa zeḡe zama mae ḡunuḡununiꞌuma, ebu ze ꞌane ḡuriro ḡoeꞌaꞌe huga radu mae ḡihiniꞌuma.
Zeꞌe ḡoere huga, hari manoḡa mene mae ḡihiniro, ebu haḡai sauꞌa sauꞌa matuꞌuḡa haḡairo. Eꞌanoꞌo Badiꞌaꞌa ꞌaheḡe ḡoreziꞌuma, ''Zaꞌe sauꞌa haḡa ahine, aduga hidiꞌuma.''
Nego nabudi, Zuhiꞌa Boro zamarone azaḡa, eme iḡaiḡa zae uꞌano Badiꞌa mazao manoḡa tauḡi raꞌohe. Mazaḡa za ꞌai ḡabozoga veize irina ꞌoma Badiꞌaꞌa inahe meiro. Aꞌe Vine Zaḡoḡaniꞌa Badiꞌa veize avo ohoziroꞌeteꞌe gauḡa uꞌano, zu zaeꞌa Badiꞌa hari manoḡa mae ḡihineꞌeteꞌe uꞌano.
Badiꞌa ani, zae ḡabodoga rae zamaziro, ebu emeḡeꞌa hari manoḡa haramoziniro. Aꞌe zae zuni Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Keriso agaḡa manoḡa zamaḡano radifine.
Eꞌanoꞌo nego nabudi, zaꞌe edau gigaranadu, emeḡeꞌa hebe hina ziroteꞌe ga fefao mirihiroteꞌe ihoreḡa ḡoeꞌa zamare radiuꞌenoꞌi!
Eme ꞌahige kuratihi: Emeḡe Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Keriso zuni Badiꞌa emeḡe Mamaꞌa zamaze rinedoꞌi, ebu haḡai manoḡa haḡaiteꞌea, zu ḡoere manoḡa reiteꞌe moneo inarazoꞌi! Badiꞌa ani emeḡe zamariro, ebu ane manoḡa uꞌano inara rifi onamo tuḡutuḡu. Kerisoꞌa emeḡe uꞌano rudaroteꞌe anoꞌo, Badiꞌaꞌa radiu tuḡutuḡu ḡauḡa rifoga veize ḡoitoriro. Ebu emeꞌa hubehune radiu tuḡutuḡu ḡauḡa zamareꞌeteꞌe hidoga veize, aniꞌa danafeꞌohe.
<range>
Nego nabudi, ḡoere ꞌahogaꞌe ꞌahiguḡa: Emeḡe veize kuranoꞌi, zaeꞌa hari manoḡa mae ḡihiniroteꞌe teige, Zuhiꞌa Boro hari manoḡaniꞌa ḡarihe rovotifine!
Ebu eme aduga rifiꞌeteꞌe azaḡa sauꞌa huneḡa mazaoꞌonoꞌo Badiꞌaꞌa eme biroga veize kuranoꞌi, mazaḡa mene vaze niduꞌaꞌe Badiꞌa mazao fieꞌohe!
Rehano Zuhiꞌa Boro aniꞌe ḡoitoroneḡa mene variꞌeꞌe ahine, aniꞌa inaraziꞌuma ebu sauꞌaniꞌa za mene meifine duguziꞌuma.
Eme hubehune ꞌahige rae zamareꞌohe: Zuhiꞌa Boroꞌa danaziꞌuma ꞌahine, emeḡeꞌa haramo ziniꞌeteꞌe haḡaiḡano zaeꞌa haḡaeꞌeteꞌe haḡaiḡaꞌe haḡae onamiꞌuma raꞌohe.
Ebu eme ꞌahige kuratihi: Zuhiꞌa Boroꞌa zamaze ibito hanadu, Badiꞌaꞌa nouge nouge zae zamare borofeꞌeteꞌe ederoga. Zu Kerisoꞌa rahao ꞌada aduga boro zamaḡano rinede onaminuteꞌe zaeꞌa ederoga, ebu zae zuni eꞌe haḡaiḡano onamoga.
Nego nabudi, Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Keriso niḡano eme ꞌahige zihi: Iesu moneo raꞌe rehano, tubuḡa azaḡa, zu emeḡeꞌa ihozidoteꞌe haḡaiḡano mene radiuꞌeteꞌe azaḡa mazaonoꞌo vaḡinoꞌi!
Zae edeḡa, emeḡeꞌa haḡaeꞌeteꞌe teige zae zuni haḡaine manoḡa. Emeḡeꞌa zae teite radiunuteꞌe madaḡano eme mene tuboga horofinu.
Eme vaze ogomu naeḡa mene haḡadu mene mae autauḡinu. Ebu za mazao aduga ꞌahoga mene zehoga veize, eme madai zu ohere gau boro haḡaido.
Emeꞌe apostolo azaḡa ꞌahine, zae mazao ogomu mae tauḡoga idaḡa rehano, emeḡeꞌa gauadu ogomu hidido. Emeḡeꞌa gau ḡihau haḡaeꞌeteꞌe zaeꞌa emeḡe haḡai horonadu, zae zuni ꞌouge haḡaifine.
Emeḡeꞌa zae teite radiunuteꞌe madaḡano zinaꞌa, ‘Iniu vaze gauoga mene uratoꞌidene, ogomu ago hanoꞌi!’ rae zido.
Emeꞌa za hari igiꞌetene, za nuꞌe tubuḡa raꞌohe. Zeꞌe mene gauadu, vaze daꞌo dudizeꞌohe.
ꞌUguḡa azaḡaꞌe, emeḡeꞌa Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Keriso niḡano ziꞌohe. Zaꞌe imuimuꞌuhi radoꞌi, ebu ogomu hidoga veize gauoꞌi!
Ebu nego nabudi, zaꞌe haḡai manoḡa haḡaeꞌeteꞌe moneo ago fuḡozoꞌi!
Iniu vazeꞌa emeḡeꞌa fefao ꞌada teateꞌe ḡoeꞌa rae modoꞌidene, eꞌe vazeḡaniꞌa nagini haḡaeꞌeteꞌe ekalesia azaḡa ihozoi! Ane teite ago zaꞌuoꞌi, ani mazagaronoga veize.
Rehano ani agire vazeḡa rae ago noꞌi, rehano negoze iraduguneꞌeteꞌe teige iradugonoꞌi!
Zama roḡeḡa rifiꞌuma Zuhiꞌaḡa Boro, aneꞌa iḡaiḡa zae radone niduꞌa zamaḡano ane zama roḡeḡa ziniꞌenoꞌi! Ebu Zuhiꞌa Boroꞌe zae niduꞌa teite radiuꞌenoꞌi!
Ḡonaga ꞌadi ḡoeꞌaꞌe eḡe, Pauloꞌa eḡe ꞌevore hina uhiu ḡoeꞌa miriheꞌohe. Aꞌe eḡeꞌa hubehune tuḡureha rae ederifine, e ꞌahige miriheꞌohe.
Emeḡe Zuhiꞌa Boro Iesu Keriso manoḡaniꞌa zae niduꞌa mazao
